int cnt

new(v1,1)

createSemaphore(cnt,rH(v1))

fork((acquire(cnt),(wH(v1,rH(v1)*10),(print(rH(v1)),release(cnt)))))

fork((acquire(cnt),(wH(v1,rH(v1)*10),(wH(v1,rH(v1)*2),(print(rH(v1)),release(cnt))))))

acquire(cnt)

print(rH(v1)-1)

createSemaphore(cnt,rH(v1))

fork((acquire(cnt),(wH(v1,rH(v1)*10),(print(rH(v1)),release(cnt)))))

fork((acquire(cnt),(wH(v1,rH(v1)*10),(wH(v1,rH(v1)*2),(print(rH(v1)),release(cnt))))))

acquire(cnt)

print(rH(v1)-1)
